His face is severely degraded: mouth frozen mid-speech with lips unnaturally locked in a single shape, teeth misaligned and crooked, deep wrinkles carved into skin like cracks, eyes dull and lifeless. He wears a layered outfit of pixelated denim jacket over a chaotic, oversaturated patterned shirt, accessories melted or missing, necklace deformed into jagged lines. His head jerks erratically — snapping forward, then lurching sideways with violent tremors, chin tilting unnaturally before snapping back, all movement broken and spasmodic. The background is a noisy collage of grainy textures, striped patterns, and floating text/logos, devoid of depth or atmosphere. Lighting is inconsistent, casting strobing highlights and deep, muddy shadows. The camera shakes violently, cuts abruptly between unframed angles, zooms erratically, and holds unstable compositions at chest level, capturing only fragmented, glitched gestures. Overall mood is jarring, broken, and disorienting — a corrupted, low-resolution 3D animation with extreme contrast, hyper-sharp edges, heavy grain, and surreal distortion, lacking any sense of calm or connection.
